type SideLength = Float in
type Height = Float in

type Shape =
  + Sphere(Radius)
  + Cube(SideLength)
  + Cylinder(Radius, Height)
in

let circumscribed_sphere_radius: Shape -> Float =
    fun shape ->
        case shape
        | Sphere(r) => r
        | Cube(l) => l / 2.0
        | Cylinder(r, h) => (h + 2.0 * r) / 4
